<!--1640697960002-->
[勇于揭露福建“政法系统教育整顿”造假联署从859人增至1010人（第三批）  ——严惩腐败人人有责，福建1000多民众冤强烈发声](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/8591010-1000.html)
------

<div>
<p><span style="font-family: 宋体;"><span></span></span></p><a name='more'></a><br /><p></p><p><span style="font-family: 宋体;">“第一批政法教育整顿，截至</span><span lang="EN-US">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">月</span><span lang="EN-US">18</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">日，福建省教育整顿办已办结群众举报线索</span><span lang="EN-US">9137</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">件，查结率达</span><span lang="EN-US">94.02%</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">，此次整顿结果得到全国教育整顿办和中央第八督导组的肯定，群众好评率达</span><span lang="EN-US">99.08%</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;">。</span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">第二批政法教育整顿，截至</span><span lang="EN-US">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">月底</span><span lang="EN-US">,</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">中央信访联席办交办我省</span><span lang="EN-US">10691</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">件重复信访事项</span><span lang="EN-US">,</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">已经化解</span><span lang="EN-US">9848</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">件</span><span lang="EN-US">,</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">占</span><span lang="EN-US">92.1%</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">。”</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">为了证实上述统计数据公开造假瞒报，福建众冤民识破政法腐败的毒瘤，将每个未查实名数据来揭开上述荒唐伪据，每次教育整顿督导组、巡视组都见不上，省政府、公安厅对他们层层保护，与访民隔绝，从何谈上查结率达</span><span lang="EN-US">94.02%</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">。</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">纵观如下未查实名众冤触目惊心，令人发指，政法腐败，巡视造假，打压维权，有法不依，有案不立，有腐不惩，有黑不除，充当保护，权钱交易，侵权渎职，徇私枉法，执法犯法，是福建执政执法的严重腐败，自受害例举名单与统计数据对照恰恰相反，众冤强烈呼吁对该伪造数据确定质疑，追责散布该虚假信息的意图罪责，背弃初心使命担当，侵害维权切身利益，践踏法律尊严，歪曲事实真相，在拆迁和政法被害的众冤，维权数年不等，甚至受害被打压成罪犯软拘囚禁，变相制造冤假错案，打击报复维权人，福建莆田欧金中就是其中最典型一例被活活逼死轰动全国，福建让谁好评？只是彰显腐败黄婆卖瓜自卖自夸，害了百姓民不聊生。</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">针对福建政法整顿屡次造假数据证明，福建众多冤民都没有解决，瞒报查结率达</span><span lang="EN-US">94.02%</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">不作为乱作为的严重腐败，实名众冤呐喊中央各上级领导高度重视和关注，对福建典型腐败造假专案督查督办，体现党的英明政策！</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">以下是网上自愿原则未查实名众冤登记名单，情况属实，众冤为真实性负法律责任，可以随时抽查核对。</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>1</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">、黄思静，女，厦门市思明区，电话</span><span lang="EN-US">15359838218</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">。</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span>2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;
